###Handling the Beam Stop Because we need to have the intensity of the image at the locations where the beam is placed to protect the detector, the values at the center of the image need to be filled in. ###Take Inverse Fourier Transform If we take the inverse Fourier transform of the symmetric image, we get the autocorrelation of the electron density.
